## Text Elements
it simply is the signed area, the fundamental theorem of calculus states that ^mml8dSF5

vectors are basically matrices with 1 column and as many rows as the dimensions ^zs2DjriH

it is not cummutative, AB is not the same as BA and the second must have 
as many rows as the columns of the first ^9fwRwJ17

a sequence where to each number a constant is added calle da common difference ^rL0Q3U7x

define a sequence as an expression involving n and needs both the expression
and the range ^fgz2aEJV

first term not in the max ^gicOT7VY

arithmetic sequences are just lines ^9vqetwuU

it is a sum of the members of a sequence ^ECLClwzu
